<review>Lived in the immediate areas my entire life and always assumed this place was only a bar. Well now I live basically across the street and I had to go check out this bay famous garlic fried chicken I've been hearing about.

We decided to go with the small bucket of garlic fried chicken that comes with 8 potato wedges which are 2 large potatoes that have been qartered. We couldn't be more pleased with what we received. The flavors of the wedges are great and last. Not like other chicken chains where it seems like you're eating straight potatoes. The chicken was heavily seasoned with garlic but surprisingly it's not overpowering at all. The garlic goes with the fried flavor perfectly. The chicken was moist and juicy and very meaty. I will be back with out a doubt . It's a very home-style joint that serves up some great comfort food and with relatively good prices.  The small bucket with 8 wedges was 16 bucks and the regular chicken is 15 I believe .<//review>< Pics>
None</Pics>

<text>Hubby says he can tell if I like a place if I'm making mmmm sounds and doing my happy dance in my seat. There was plenty of that going around during our visit tonight.

<Name>Lynn Lee< /Name>< review>
I saw Dr. Patterson for a root canal today and I must say I was very, very nervous initially due to my experience with a failed root canal attempt with another dentist at another location a couple weeks earlier.   However, after speaking with Dr. Patterson, I elected to move forward with the root canal.  He explained everything and allowed me the opportunity to process the information given and to decide on my options.

Dr. Patterson and his assistant, Christine were both very nice and professional.  Christine had such a calm and caring demeanor.

Christine put on the classical music I chose to listen to for my ear piece and the rest is history. No pain and it was over in less than 30 minutes.  I literally fell asleep during the entire procedure and was not under general anesthesia.

If you have a fear of dentist and not a fan of root canals, you must see Dr. Patterson and the dental staff at Rancho Endodontics.  They honestly know what they are doing.  Dr. Patterson is the guy.

Awesome experience!!!<//review>

I'm going to give this particular Romano's Mac Grill a 5 star bordering on 4 tbh. 5 only bc the wait staff was very nice and extremely hard working. This particular night was semi busy. The staff worked off of each other making sure the customers were well taken care of even if they were passing by another staff's table. Very friendly and warming from all of them. And considering it was outdoors, the staff did thier best to keep our cups full.

I found it unusual that they didn't have menus and we had to look at our phones to look at thier website to see the menu. I don't particularly care for this system.

The food was pretty good for a chain restaurant. I opted for the Trio Plate and the Bisque as a starter. The Bisque was a tad salty. I was offered another bowl but felt I already had to much sodium for the night. The Trio which consisted of Fettuccine Alfredo 8/10, Lasagna7/10, and a Chicken Marsala was decent 6/10 (it was kinda burnt). I was happy my plate came out nice and hot. My daughter had the Spaghetti and meatballs. It tasted decently good as well. 8/10.

I'd probably go back again. If I do I'll give it another review update</text>

On the other hand, the food was not so good. The bread had a good flavor but it was overwhelmingly salty. I ordered the butternut tortellacci. Honestly, with a small fraction of the salt this would probably be pretty good. It has prosciutto in it, which is already salty, so it really wasn't necessary to load it up. It totally smothered the flavor of everything else and left me with that heavy, bloated, sodium overload feeling like I just ate at Macdonald's.

My husband ordered the chicken fettuccine alfredo. It's hard to mess that up. The pasta was alright, but the chicken was both sparse and extremely poor in quality. He regretted eating it and didn't feel well afterward. So about $4 to add that gross chicken to a $13 plate of plain pasta. Not a huge plate.

< Text>
I drive UberEats regularly and pickup from this Macaroni Grill pretty often. It always has alot of customers inside, but my wait for the takeout has always been just a couple of minutes until last nite. Took about 20 minutes as they were slammed. There was another UberEats driver in addition to the other delivery service drivers there, HubGrub & ? and there were also 4 customers that called in their orders for carry out.  The staff moved things along as quickly as they could to get each of us taken care of and on our way throwing in an extra something here and there or reducing the prices slightly to make up for the wait. It wasn't necessary as anyone that has ever eaten here should be aware that a busy restaurant means some amount of wait time due to the quality of food. The woman handling the orders (Yvonne) kept her composure as did the Manager (Can't remember his name). He gave me 2 different plates, a Chicken Alfredo and Lasagne for my wait. As I  said. they do see me as I said, quite often and maybe this was the reason. Both were very tasty and it was a nice gesture on his part. Now having tasted their food, I understand why the place always has alot of customers every time I'm sent there to pick up an order and I'll be taking my wife out to dinner here having sampled a very small portion of their menu. Tasty & Much appreciated.< /Text>

<pictures>None< /pictures>< review>
The Macaroni Grill on Grand Oaks, Corona Ca has the WORST customer service ever. Unfortunately for us, we gave them a second chance and went there tonight. Big mistake.

My family and I (2 adults, 2 kids) were seated in the bar area, not our choice. We arrived at 7PM and waited 25 minutes, not too bad. The restaurant was extremely busy for a Friday night, first week in November.

We waited several minutes for someone to take our drink/appetizer order. Appetizers came out quick, but no silverware to eat with. By the time we got silverware, the appetizers were cold.

Eventually the bartender (cause he was the only one handling the entire bar and tables within) came to take our order, and immediately realized we never got our drinks. He took our order and returned with our drinks.

Once the food was delivered, our table was never visited again except to drop off the bill. No drink refills, no parmesan cheese to top our entre's, nothing. My wife had to visit the hostess counter on two different occasions to inquire about drink refills and bread.

There appeared to be two managers on staff tonight. We tried to get their attention as they passed by our table, (walking together deep in a conversation) it was as if what they were talking about was much more important than a paying customer who's bill was north of $80 for 4 people.

Ideally we would like our money back, but it's our fault for not leaving during the drink/appetizer debacle.

The irony is, out of all the other restaurants we frequent in (or near) the Corona Crossings Shopping center, (Kings Fish House, Wood Ranch, Miguels, Chilis, BJ's Pizza...etc), they all seem to handle a busy crowd, but for some odd reason, Macaroni Grill fails every time.

We wont be back. (Unless they read this and comp our meal, we did save our receipt)<//review>

We can sum it up 3 words, OVERPRICED AND UNDERWHELMING. I had the Carmena Chicken with a house salad, ok so what they should have put in the description is" a bowl full of greasy sauceless rigatoni that a heavy dose of salt and parmesan could not fix. Hubby had the 3 course dinner with the mac and cheese bites, pork shank and chocolate cake which translates into 4 squares of flavorless noodles deep fried with some tasteless sauce which we could not figure out what the flavor was supposed to be, a pan of overcooked potatoes, some carrots for color and a hunk of bone with some meat on the outside oh and the marsala sauce that tasted like it came out of a healthy choice box, now lets not forget the dessert that said chocolate cake but looked more like a flat cupcake with some stuff on it that tasted like oil and sugar frosting. The ultimate bellini drink was not named properly as it was more like syrup under a slushi and the always hot out of the oven bread which the waitress forgot to bring until we asked for it was just salty coated bread with olive oil that was turning sour. Overall definitely not worth the 80 dollar total with tip and when the manager in the prince purple shirt asked how was everything and we said OK you would think he would inquire as to what could have made it better but no he just walked away.
